  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jRpzNofg7wf89Xx+uplBaVI2rz2M7py7B870MLVO1/I2PAnJiI27tsjFM1cBigPMqHuXcJd+dD7Pw326y4Kd2Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w1BZGpQhngaYpU+r+s7YPgvqsTulJunvTymXbn87hUZ4diPlm0zKt6yVAIJB3Zqb8aeJdr62AWqHJB7kAffPbQ==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/85634.Brian_Malloy">About Brian Malloy</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/85634.Brian_Malloy"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1600709563p3/85634.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/85634.Brian_Malloy">Brian Malloy
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
40
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13670260496458699805">A dual national of the United States and Ireland, Brian was born in Philadelphia and grew up in Pennsylvania, Illinois, Missouri, Michigan, and Pennsylvania (again). Minneapolis has been - more or less - his home since 1978 (with a few years here and there in D.C., Amsterdam, and Boston). He was an early employee of the Minnesota AIDS Project (now JustUs Health) in the 1980s, a volunteer with the </span>
  <span id="freeText13670260496458699805" style="display:none">A dual national of the United States and Ireland, Brian was born in Philadelphia and grew up in Pennsylvania, Illinois, Missouri, Michigan, and Pennsylvania (again). Minneapolis has been - more or less - his home since 1978 (with a few years here and there in D.C., Amsterdam, and Boston). He was an early employee of the Minnesota AIDS Project (now JustUs Health) in the 1980s, a volunteer with the 1987 Minnesota March on Washington for Lesbian &amp; Gay Rights, and the volunteer coordinator for Minnesota's first AIDS walk in 1988.<br /><br /><br />In the 1990s, Brian founded and secured matching funds for the Minnesota Lesbian &amp; Gay Community Funding Partnership, a three-year initiative to expand funding opportunities to Minnesota's LGBT community. The Minnesota Partnership was part of The National Lesbian and Gay Community Funding Partnership, and awarded over $400,000 for LGBT services across the state. <br /><br /><br />Brian was part of the team that founded Open Book, the permanent home of The Loft Literary Center, Milkweed Editions, and the Minnesota Center for Book Arts. Brian served as the grant writer for the successful capital campaign.<br /><br /><br />In the 2000s, Brian launched the Loft Literary Center's first writing conferences for writers of mysteries and thrillers, for comic book and graphic novel writers and illustrators, for older adult writers, for teen writers, and for nature and environmental writers. During his tenure at the Loft, City Pages honored the organization with its Best Writing Classes award, beating out the region's university-based creative writing programs.<br /><br /><br />Currently, Brian is self-employed as a grant writing consultant, grant reviewer, adjunct instructor, and teaching artist. He is a proud member of the Service Employees International Union, Local 284.<br /><br />Brian has been married (illegally and legally) to his husband for over 30 years, and they are the proud parents of rescue dogs. <br /><br />Brian supports Friends of the Boundary Waters, a campaign to ban copper sulfide mining in the Boundary Waters Canoe Area Wilderness Watershed and the Lake Superior Watershed.<br /><br />Brian is not on Twitter, Instagram, Snapchat, TikTok, Pinterest, Reddit, or other social media sites, so this is not the Brian Malloy who made you so mad. He does have a Facebook Page for Brian Malloy, Novelist. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13670260496458699805" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
